Descrição: Ensure all skip links have a focusable target
Sugestão: The skip-link target should exist and be focusable
Mais informações: https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.10/skip-link?application=axeAPI
Tags: cat.keyboard, best-practice
  - Elemento: a[href$="#main-searchbox"]
    Código: <a class="br-item" href="#main-searchbox" role="menuitem" accesskey="3">Ir para a busca <span aria-hidden="true">(3/4)</span> <span aria-hidden="true" class="br-tag text ml-1">3</span></a>
  - Elemento: a[href$="#footer"]
    Código: <a class="br-item" href="#footer" role="menuitem" accesskey="4">Ir para o rodapé <span aria-hidden="true">(4/4)</span> <span aria-hidden="true" class="br-tag text ml-1">4</span></a>
